## ğŸ¯ **1. å½¢å¼åŒ–è¯æ˜åŸºç¡€ / Formal Proof Fundamentals**

### 1.1 è¯æ˜ç³»ç»Ÿ / Proof Systems

**å®šä¹‰ 1.1** (å½¢å¼åŒ–è¯æ˜ç³»ç»Ÿ / Formal Proof System)
**å½¢å¼åŒ–è¯æ˜ç³»ç»Ÿ**æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªå››å…ƒç»„ï¼Œç”¨äºä¸¥æ ¼éªŒè¯æ•°å­¦å‘½é¢˜çš„æ­£ç¡®æ€§ï¼š
$$P = (L, A, R, T)$$
å…¶ä¸­ï¼š

- $L$ æ˜¯**å½¢å¼è¯­è¨€**ï¼ˆformal languageï¼‰ï¼Œå®šä¹‰ç¬¦å·å’Œè¯­æ³•
- $A$ æ˜¯**å…¬ç†é›†**ï¼ˆaxiom setï¼‰ï¼ŒåŸºæœ¬å‡è®¾
- $R$ æ˜¯**æ¨ç†è§„åˆ™é›†**ï¼ˆinference rule setï¼‰ï¼Œæ¨å¯¼è§„åˆ™
- $T$ æ˜¯**å®šç†é›†**ï¼ˆtheorem setï¼‰ï¼Œå¯è¯æ˜çš„å‘½é¢˜

**å†å²èƒŒæ™¯**ï¼š

- **å¤å¸Œè…Š**ï¼šæ¬§å‡ é‡Œå¾—ã€Šå‡ ä½•åŸæœ¬ã€‹å»ºç«‹å…¬ç†åŒ–æ–¹æ³•
- **19ä¸–çºª**ï¼šå¸ƒå°”ä»£æ•°ã€é›†åˆè®ºå‘å±•
- **20ä¸–çºªåˆ**ï¼šå¸Œå°”ä¼¯ç‰¹å½¢å¼åŒ–æ•°å­¦è®¡åˆ’
- **1930å¹´ä»£**ï¼šå“¥å¾·å°”ä¸å®Œå¤‡å®šç†
- **1960å¹´ä»£**ï¼šè‡ªåŠ¨å®šç†è¯æ˜å…´èµ·
- **2000å¹´ä»£**ï¼šè®¡ç®—æœºè¾…åŠ©è¯æ˜å‘å±•

**åº”ç”¨é¢†åŸŸ**ï¼š

- **æ•°å­¦**ï¼šå®šç†è¯æ˜ã€æ•°å­¦å‘ç°
- **è®¡ç®—æœºç§‘å­¦**ï¼šç¨‹åºéªŒè¯ã€ç®—æ³•æ­£ç¡®æ€§
- **äººå·¥æ™ºèƒ½**ï¼šè‡ªåŠ¨æ¨ç†ã€çŸ¥è¯†è¡¨ç¤º
- **å“²å­¦**ï¼šé€»è¾‘å­¦ã€è®¤è¯†è®º

### 1.2 è¯æ˜ä¸å®šç† / Proofs and Theorems

**å®šä¹‰ 1.2** (è¯æ˜ / Proof)
**è¯æ˜**æ˜¯ä»å…¬ç†åˆ°å®šç†çš„æœ‰é™æ­¥éª¤åºåˆ—ï¼š
$$\pi = (\phi_1, \phi_2, \ldots, \phi_n)$$
å…¶ä¸­æ¯ä¸ª $\phi_i$ è¦ä¹ˆæ˜¯å…¬ç†ï¼Œè¦ä¹ˆç”±å‰é¢çš„å…¬å¼é€šè¿‡æ¨ç†è§„åˆ™å¾—åˆ°ã€‚

**å®šä¹‰ 1.3** (å®šç† / Theorem)
**å®šç†**æ˜¯å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡è¯æ˜ä»å…¬ç†æ¨å¯¼å‡ºçš„å…¬å¼ï¼š
$$\phi \in T \iff \exists \pi: \text{proof}(\pi, \phi)$$

**è¯æ˜ç±»å‹**ï¼š

- **æ„é€ æ€§è¯æ˜**ï¼šç›´æ¥æ„é€ è¯æ˜å¯¹è±¡
- **å­˜åœ¨æ€§è¯æ˜**ï¼šè¯æ˜å­˜åœ¨æ€§ä½†ä¸æ„é€ 
- **åè¯æ³•**ï¼šé€šè¿‡çŸ›ç›¾è¯æ˜
- **å½’çº³è¯æ˜**ï¼šæ•°å­¦å½’çº³æ³•
- **å¯¹å¶è¯æ˜**ï¼šåˆ©ç”¨å¯¹å¶æ€§

### 1.3 é€»è¾‘ç³»ç»Ÿ / Logical Systems

**å®šä¹‰ 1.4** (å‘½é¢˜é€»è¾‘ / Propositional Logic)
**å‘½é¢˜é€»è¾‘**æ˜¯åŸºæœ¬çš„é€»è¾‘ç³»ç»Ÿï¼š
$$L_P = (V, O, F)$$
å…¶ä¸­ï¼š

- $V$ æ˜¯**å‘½é¢˜å˜é‡é›†**ï¼ˆpropositional variablesï¼‰
- $O = \{\neg, \land, \lor, \to, \leftrightarrow\}$ æ˜¯**é€»è¾‘è¿ç®—ç¬¦**ï¼ˆlogical operatorsï¼‰
- $F$ æ˜¯**å…¬å¼é›†**ï¼ˆformula setï¼‰

**å®šä¹‰ 1.5** (ä¸€é˜¶é€»è¾‘ / First-Order Logic)
**ä¸€é˜¶é€»è¾‘**æ‰©å±•å‘½é¢˜é€»è¾‘ï¼š
$$L_F = (V, C, F, P, Q)$$
å…¶ä¸­ï¼š

- $V$ æ˜¯**å˜é‡é›†**ï¼ˆvariable setï¼‰
- $C$ æ˜¯**å¸¸é‡é›†**ï¼ˆconstant setï¼‰
- $F$ æ˜¯**å‡½æ•°ç¬¦å·é›†**ï¼ˆfunction symbol setï¼‰
- $P$ æ˜¯**è°“è¯ç¬¦å·é›†**ï¼ˆpredicate symbol setï¼‰
- $Q = \{\forall, \exists\}$ æ˜¯**é‡è¯**ï¼ˆquantifiersï¼‰

**é€»è¾‘ç³»ç»Ÿç±»å‹**ï¼š

- **ç»å…¸é€»è¾‘**ï¼šäºŒå€¼é€»è¾‘
- **ç›´è§‰é€»è¾‘**ï¼šæ„é€ æ€§é€»è¾‘
- **æ¨¡æ€é€»è¾‘**ï¼šå¯èƒ½æ€§å’Œå¿…ç„¶æ€§
- **æ—¶æ€é€»è¾‘**ï¼šæ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³é€»è¾‘
- **æ¨¡ç³Šé€»è¾‘**ï¼šå¤šå€¼é€»è¾‘

## ğŸ” **2. è¯æ˜æ–¹æ³• / Proof Methods**

### 2.0 è¯æ˜æ–¹æ³•å¯¹æ¯”çŸ©é˜µ / Proof Methods Comparison Matrix

| è¯æ˜æ–¹æ³• | é€‚ç”¨åœºæ™¯ | è¯æ˜ç­–ç•¥ | ä¼˜ç‚¹ | ç¼ºç‚¹ | å…¸å‹åº”ç”¨ |
|---------|---------|---------|------|------|---------|
| **ç›´æ¥è¯æ˜** | å‰ææ˜ç¡®ï¼Œç»“è®ºå¯ç›´æ¥æ¨å¯¼ | ä»å‰æé€æ­¥æ¨å¯¼ | ç›´è§‚ã€æ¸…æ™° | éœ€è¦æ˜ç¡®çš„æ¨ç†è·¯å¾„ | ç­‰å¼è¯æ˜ã€ä¸ç­‰å¼è¯æ˜ |
| **åè¯æ³•** | ç›´æ¥è¯æ˜å›°éš¾ï¼Œå¦å®šç»“è®ºæ˜“å¾—çŸ›ç›¾ | å‡è®¾ç»“è®ºå¦å®šï¼Œæ¨å¯¼çŸ›ç›¾ | æ€è·¯æ¸…æ™°ï¼Œé€‚åˆå­˜åœ¨æ€§è¯æ˜ | éœ€è¦æ‰¾åˆ°åˆé€‚çš„çŸ›ç›¾ | å”¯ä¸€æ€§è¯æ˜ã€å­˜åœ¨æ€§è¯æ˜ |
| **æ•°å­¦å½’çº³æ³•** | å…³äºè‡ªç„¶æ•°çš„å‘½é¢˜ | åŸºç¡€æƒ…å†µ+å½’çº³æ­¥éª¤ | ç³»ç»Ÿæ€§å¼ºï¼Œé€‚åˆé€’å½’ç»“æ„ | éœ€è¦æ‰¾åˆ°åˆé€‚çš„å½’çº³å‡è®¾ | æ•°åˆ—ã€ç®—æ³•æ­£ç¡®æ€§ |
| **ç»“æ„å½’çº³æ³•** | é€’å½’å®šä¹‰çš„ç»“æ„ | åŸºç¡€æƒ…å†µ+æ„é€ æ­¥éª¤ | é€‚åˆé€’å½’æ•°æ®ç»“æ„ | éœ€è¦ç†è§£ç»“æ„å®šä¹‰ | æ ‘ã€åˆ—è¡¨ã€è¡¨è¾¾å¼ |
| **æ„é€ æ€§è¯æ˜** | å­˜åœ¨æ€§è¯æ˜ | ç›´æ¥æ„é€ å¯¹è±¡ | æä¾›å…·ä½“å¯¹è±¡ | æ„é€ å¯èƒ½å¤æ‚ | ç®—æ³•å­˜åœ¨æ€§ã€è§£çš„å­˜åœ¨æ€§ |
| **å¯¹å¶è¯æ˜** | æœ‰å¯¹å¶æ€§è´¨çš„é—®é¢˜ | åˆ©ç”¨å¯¹å¶æ€§ | ç®€åŒ–è¯æ˜ | éœ€è¦è¯†åˆ«å¯¹å¶æ€§ | å›¾è®ºã€ä¼˜åŒ–é—®é¢˜ |
| **åŒè®¡æ•°åŸç†** | è®¡æ•°é—®é¢˜ | ä»ä¸¤ä¸ªè§’åº¦è®¡æ•° | ç®€æ´æœ‰åŠ› | éœ€è¦æ‰¾åˆ°åˆé€‚çš„è®¡æ•°æ–¹å¼ | ç»„åˆæ•°å­¦ã€å›¾è®º |

### 2.1 ç›´æ¥è¯æ˜ / Direct Proof

**å®šä¹‰ 2.1** (ç›´æ¥è¯æ˜ / Direct Proof)
**ç›´æ¥è¯æ˜**æ˜¯ä»å‰æç›´æ¥æ¨å¯¼ç»“è®ºçš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼š
$$\text{premises} \vdash \text{conclusion}$$

**ç®—æ³• 2.1** (ç›´æ¥è¯æ˜ç®—æ³• / Direct Proof Algorithm)

```python
class DirectProof:
    def __init__(self, premises, conclusion):
        self.premises = premises
        self.conclusion = conclusion
        self.proof_steps = []

    def prove(self):
        """æ‰§è¡Œç›´æ¥è¯æ˜"""
        current_goal = self.conclusion
        available_facts = set(self.premises)

        while current_goal not in available_facts:
            # é€‰æ‹©æ¨ç†è§„åˆ™
            rule = self.select_rule(current_goal)
            if not rule:
                raise Exception("æ— æ³•æ‰¾åˆ°åˆé€‚çš„æ¨ç†è§„åˆ™")

            # åº”ç”¨è§„åˆ™
            subgoals = self.apply_rule(rule, current_goal)
            self.proof_steps.append({
                'rule': rule,
                'goal': current_goal,
                'subgoals': subgoals
            })

            # æ›´æ–°å¯ç”¨äº‹å®å’Œç›®æ ‡
            for subgoal in subgoals:
                if subgoal in available_facts:
                    available_facts.add(current_goal)
                    break
            else:
                # é€’å½’è¯æ˜å­ç›®æ ‡
                for subgoal in subgoals:
                    if subgoal not in available_facts:
                        current_goal = subgoal
                        break

        return self.proof_steps

    def select_rule(self, goal):
        """é€‰æ‹©æ¨ç†è§„åˆ™"""
        # æ ¹æ®ç›®æ ‡ç±»å‹é€‰æ‹©è§„åˆ™
        if isinstance(goal, Implication):
            return "implication_introduction"
        elif isinstance(goal, Conjunction):
            return "conjunction_introduction"
        elif isinstance(goal, Disjunction):
            return "disjunction_introduction"
        return None

    def apply_rule(self, rule, goal):
        """åº”ç”¨æ¨ç†è§„åˆ™"""
        if rule == "implication_introduction":
            return [goal.antecedent, goal.consequent]
        elif rule == "conjunction_introduction":
            return [goal.left, goal.right]
        elif rule == "disjunction_introduction":
            return [goal.left]  # æˆ– goal.right
        return []
```

**ç¤ºä¾‹ 2.1** (ç›´æ¥è¯æ˜ç¤ºä¾‹)

```python
# è¯æ˜ï¼šå¦‚æœ p ä¸” qï¼Œåˆ™ p
premises = [Conjunction("p", "q")]
conclusion = Implication(Conjunction("p", "q"), "p")

proof = DirectProof(premises, conclusion)
steps = proof.prove()
print("è¯æ˜æ­¥éª¤ï¼š", steps)
```

### 2.2 åè¯æ³• / Proof by Contradiction

**å®šä¹‰ 2.2** (åè¯æ³• / Proof by Contradiction)
**åè¯æ³•**é€šè¿‡å‡è®¾ç»“è®ºçš„å¦å®šæ¥è¯æ˜åŸç»“è®ºï¼š
$$\text{premises} \cup \{\neg \phi\} \vdash \bot \implies \text{premises} \vdash \phi$$

**ç®—æ³• 2.2** (åè¯æ³•ç®—æ³• / Contradiction Proof Algorithm)

```python
class ContradictionProof:
    def __init__(self, premises, conclusion):
        self.premises = premises
        self.conclusion = conclusion
        self.proof_steps = []

    def prove(self):
        """æ‰§è¡Œåè¯æ³•è¯æ˜"""
        # å‡è®¾ç»“è®ºçš„å¦å®š
        negated_conclusion = Negation(self.conclusion)
        extended_premises = self.premises + [negated_conclusion]

        try:
            # å°è¯•ä»æ‰©å±•å‰ææ¨å¯¼çŸ›ç›¾
            contradiction = self.derive_contradiction(extended_premises)

            # åº”ç”¨å¦å®šå¼•å…¥è§„åˆ™
            self.proof_steps.append({
                'method': 'contradiction',
                'assumption': negated_conclusion,
                'contradiction': contradiction,
                'conclusion': self.conclusion
            })

            return self.proof_steps

        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"åè¯æ³•å¤±è´¥ï¼š{e}")

    def derive_contradiction(self, premises):
        """æ¨å¯¼çŸ›ç›¾"""
        # ä½¿ç”¨ç›´æ¥è¯æ˜æ–¹æ³•å¯»æ‰¾çŸ›ç›¾
        proof_engine = DirectProof(premises, Contradiction())
        return proof_engine.prove()

    def apply_negation_introduction(self, assumption, contradiction):
        """åº”ç”¨å¦å®šå¼•å…¥è§„åˆ™"""
        # ä»å‡è®¾å’ŒçŸ›ç›¾æ¨å¯¼åŸç»“è®º
        return {
            'rule': 'negation_introduction',
            'assumption': assumption,
            'contradiction': contradiction,
            'conclusion': Negation(assumption)
        }
```

**ç¤ºä¾‹ 2.2** (åè¯æ³•ç¤ºä¾‹)

```python
# è¯æ˜ï¼šâˆš2 æ˜¯æ— ç†æ•°
premises = [
    "âˆš2 = p/q where p,q are coprime integers",
    "pÂ² = 2qÂ²",
    "p is even",
    "q is even"
]
conclusion = "âˆš2 is irrational"

proof = ContradictionProof(premises, conclusion)
steps = proof.prove()
print("åè¯æ³•æ­¥éª¤ï¼š", steps)
```

### 2.3 å½’çº³è¯æ˜ / Inductive Proof

**å®šä¹‰ 2.3** (æ•°å­¦å½’çº³æ³• / Mathematical Induction)
**æ•°å­¦å½’çº³æ³•**ç”¨äºè¯æ˜å…³äºè‡ªç„¶æ•°çš„å‘½é¢˜ï¼š
$$\text{Base}: P(0) \land \text{Step}: \forall n (P(n) \to P(n+1)) \implies \forall n P(n)$$

**ç®—æ³• 2.3** (æ•°å­¦å½’çº³æ³•ç®—æ³• / Mathematical Induction Algorithm)

```python
class MathematicalInduction:
    def __init__(self, predicate, base_case, inductive_step):
        self.predicate = predicate
        self.base_case = base_case
        self.inductive_step = inductive_step
        self.proof_steps = []

    def prove(self):
        """æ‰§è¡Œæ•°å­¦å½’çº³æ³•è¯æ˜"""
        # æ­¥éª¤1ï¼šè¯æ˜åŸºç¡€æƒ…å†µ
        base_proof = self.prove_base_case()
        self.proof_steps.append({
            'step': 'base_case',
            'proof': base_proof
        })

        # æ­¥éª¤2ï¼šè¯æ˜å½’çº³æ­¥éª¤
        inductive_proof = self.prove_inductive_step()
        self.proof_steps.append({
            'step': 'inductive_step',
            'proof': inductive_proof
        })

        # æ­¥éª¤3ï¼šåº”ç”¨å½’çº³åŸç†
        self.proof_steps.append({
            'step': 'induction_principle',
            'conclusion': f"âˆ€n {self.predicate}(n)"
        })

        return self.proof_steps

    def prove_base_case(self):
        """è¯æ˜åŸºç¡€æƒ…å†µ P(0)"""
        return DirectProof([], self.base_case).prove()

    def prove_inductive_step(self):
        """è¯æ˜å½’çº³æ­¥éª¤ âˆ€n (P(n) â†’ P(n+1))"""
        # å‡è®¾ P(n) æˆç«‹
        assumption = self.predicate("n")
        # è¯æ˜ P(n+1) æˆç«‹
        conclusion = self.predicate("n+1")

        return DirectProof([assumption], conclusion).prove()
```

**ç¤ºä¾‹ 2.3** (æ•°å­¦å½’çº³æ³•ç¤ºä¾‹)

```python
# è¯æ˜ï¼š1 + 2 + ... + n = n(n+1)/2
def sum_formula(n):
    return f"sum(1 to {n}) = {n}({n}+1)/2"

# åŸºç¡€æƒ…å†µï¼šn = 1
base_case = "sum(1 to 1) = 1(1+1)/2 = 1"

# å½’çº³æ­¥éª¤ï¼šå‡è®¾ sum(1 to n) = n(n+1)/2ï¼Œè¯æ˜ sum(1 to n+1) = (n+1)(n+2)/2
inductive_step = "sum(1 to n+1) = sum(1 to n) + (n+1) = n(n+1)/2 + (n+1) = (n+1)(n+2)/2"

proof = MathematicalInduction(sum_formula, base_case, inductive_step)
steps = proof.prove()
print("å½’çº³è¯æ˜æ­¥éª¤ï¼š", steps)
```

### 2.4 ç»“æ„å½’çº³æ³• / Structural Induction

**å®šç† 2.4.1** (ç»“æ„å½’çº³æ³•æ­£ç¡®æ€§ / Structural Induction Correctness)
ç»“æ„å½’çº³æ³•èƒ½å¤Ÿæ­£ç¡®è¯æ˜å…³äºé€’å½’å®šä¹‰ç»“æ„çš„å‘½é¢˜ã€‚

**å½¢å¼åŒ–è¯æ˜ / Formal Proof**ï¼š

**æ­¥éª¤ 1**ï¼šç»“æ„å®šä¹‰
è®¾ç»“æ„ç±»å‹ $T$ ç”±ä»¥ä¸‹è§„åˆ™é€’å½’å®šä¹‰ï¼š

- **åŸºç¡€æƒ…å†µ**ï¼š$B_1, B_2, \ldots, B_k$ æ˜¯ $T$ çš„åŸºç¡€å…ƒç´ 
- **æ„é€ è§„åˆ™**ï¼šå¦‚æœ $t_1, t_2, \ldots, t_n \in T$ï¼Œåˆ™ $C(t_1, t_2, \ldots, t_n) \in T$

**æ­¥éª¤ 2**ï¼šå½’çº³åŸç†
è¦è¯æ˜ $\forall t \in T: P(t)$ï¼Œéœ€è¦ï¼š

1. **åŸºç¡€æƒ…å†µ**ï¼šè¯æ˜ $P(B_i)$ å¯¹æ‰€æœ‰åŸºç¡€å…ƒç´  $B_i$ æˆç«‹
2. **å½’çº³æ­¥éª¤**ï¼šè¯æ˜å¦‚æœ $P(t_1), P(t_2), \ldots, P(t_n)$ æˆç«‹ï¼Œåˆ™ $P(C(t_1, t_2, \ldots, t_n))$ æˆç«‹

**æ­¥éª¤ 3**ï¼šæœ€å°æ€§
ç”±äº $T$ æ˜¯é€’å½’å®šä¹‰çš„ï¼Œ$T$ ä¸­çš„æ¯ä¸ªå…ƒç´ éƒ½å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡æœ‰é™æ¬¡åº”ç”¨æ„é€ è§„åˆ™ä»åŸºç¡€å…ƒç´ å¾—åˆ°ã€‚

**æ­¥éª¤ 4**ï¼šå½’çº³è¯æ˜
ä½¿ç”¨æ•°å­¦å½’çº³æ³•è¯æ˜ï¼šå¯¹äºä»»æ„ $t \in T$ï¼Œå¦‚æœ $t$ å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡ $k$ æ¬¡æ„é€ å¾—åˆ°ï¼Œåˆ™ $P(t)$ æˆç«‹ã€‚

**åŸºç¡€æƒ…å†µ**ï¼ˆ$k = 0$ï¼‰ï¼š$t$ æ˜¯åŸºç¡€å…ƒç´ ï¼Œç”±æ­¥éª¤ 2 çš„åŸºç¡€æƒ…å†µï¼Œ$P(t)$ æˆç«‹ã€‚

**å½’çº³æ­¥éª¤**ï¼šå‡è®¾å¯¹äºæ‰€æœ‰å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡ $k$ æ¬¡æ„é€ å¾—åˆ°çš„å…ƒç´  $t$ï¼Œ$P(t)$ æˆç«‹ã€‚å¯¹äºå¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡ $k+1$ æ¬¡æ„é€ å¾—åˆ°çš„å…ƒç´  $t = C(t_1, t_2, \ldots, t_n)$ï¼Œå…¶ä¸­ $t_1, t_2, \ldots, t_n$ å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡æœ€å¤š $k$ æ¬¡æ„é€ å¾—åˆ°ï¼Œç”±å½’çº³å‡è®¾å’Œæ­¥éª¤ 2 çš„å½’çº³æ­¥éª¤ï¼Œ$P(t)$ æˆç«‹ã€‚

**æ­¥éª¤ 5**ï¼šç»“è®º
å› æ­¤ï¼Œ$\forall t \in T: P(t)$ æˆç«‹ã€‚$\square$

**å®šä¹‰ 2.4** (ç»“æ„å½’çº³æ³• / Structural Induction)
**ç»“æ„å½’çº³æ³•**ç”¨äºè¯æ˜å…³äºé€’å½’å®šä¹‰ç»“æ„çš„å‘½é¢˜ï¼š
$$\text{Base}: P(\text{base cases}) \land \text{Step}: P(\text{components}) \to P(\text{constructed}) \implies \forall x P(x)$$

**ç®—æ³• 2.4** (ç»“æ„å½’çº³æ³•ç®—æ³• / Structural Induction Algorithm)

```python
class StructuralInduction:
    def __init__(self, structure_type, predicate):
        self.structure_type = structure_type
        self.predicate = predicate
        self.proof_steps = []

    def prove(self, structure):
        """æ‰§è¡Œç»“æ„å½’çº³æ³•è¯æ˜"""
        if self.is_base_case(structure):
            return self.prove_base_case(structure)
        else:
            # é€’å½’è¯æ˜å­ç»“æ„
            sub_proofs = []
            for component in self.get_components(structure):
                sub_proof = self.prove(component)
                sub_proofs.append(sub_proof)

            # è¯æ˜æ„é€ æ­¥éª¤
            construction_proof = self.prove_construction(structure, sub_proofs)

            return {
                'structure': structure,
                'sub_proofs': sub_proofs,
                'construction_proof': construction_proof
            }

    def is_base_case(self, structure):
        """åˆ¤æ–­æ˜¯å¦ä¸ºåŸºæœ¬æƒ…å†µ"""
        return len(self.get_components(structure)) == 0

    def get_components(self, structure):
        """è·å–ç»“æ„çš„ç»„æˆéƒ¨åˆ†"""
        # æ ¹æ®ç»“æ„ç±»å‹è¿”å›ç»„æˆéƒ¨åˆ†
        if isinstance(structure, list):
            return structure[:-1] if len(structure) > 1 else []
        elif isinstance(structure, tree):
            return structure.children
        return []
```

```text
è¾“å…¥ï¼šå‘½é¢˜ P(n)ï¼Œè‡ªç„¶æ•° n
è¾“å‡ºï¼šè¯æ˜åºåˆ—

1. åŸºç¡€æƒ…å†µï¼šprove P(0)
2. å½’çº³æ­¥éª¤ï¼šassume P(k) for arbitrary k
3. è¯æ˜ P(k+1)ï¼šprove P(k+1) using P(k)
4. åº”ç”¨å½’çº³ï¼šapply_induction()
5. è¿”å›è¯æ˜ï¼šreturn proof
```

## ğŸ¤– **3. è‡ªåŠ¨å®šç†è¯æ˜ / Automated Theorem Proving**

### 3.0 è‡ªåŠ¨å®šç†è¯æ˜æ–¹æ³•å¯¹æ¯”çŸ©é˜µ / Automated Theorem Proving Methods Comparison Matrix

| æ–¹æ³• | é€»è¾‘ç³»ç»Ÿ | æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ | ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ | ä¼˜ç‚¹ | ç¼ºç‚¹ | å…¸å‹åº”ç”¨ |
|------|---------|-----------|-----------|------|------|---------|
| **å½’ç»“åŸç†** | ä¸€é˜¶é€»è¾‘ | æŒ‡æ•°æ—¶é—´ | æŒ‡æ•°ç©ºé—´ | å®Œå¤‡ã€ç³»ç»ŸåŒ– | ç»„åˆçˆ†ç‚¸ | é€»è¾‘æ¨ç†ã€çŸ¥è¯†åº“ |
| **è¡¨æ–¹æ³•** | ä¸€é˜¶é€»è¾‘ | æŒ‡æ•°æ—¶é—´ | æŒ‡æ•°ç©ºé—´ | ç›´è§‚ã€ç³»ç»ŸåŒ– | ç»„åˆçˆ†ç‚¸ | é€»è¾‘æ¨ç†ã€è¯æ˜æœç´¢ |
| **æ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹** | æ—¶æ€é€»è¾‘ | å¤šé¡¹å¼æ—¶é—´ | å¤šé¡¹å¼ç©ºé—´ | è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–ã€é«˜æ•ˆ | çŠ¶æ€ç©ºé—´çˆ†ç‚¸ | ç¡¬ä»¶éªŒè¯ã€åè®®éªŒè¯ |
| **äº¤äº’å¼è¯æ˜** | é«˜é˜¶é€»è¾‘ | ä¾èµ–ç”¨æˆ· | å¤šé¡¹å¼ç©ºé—´ | çµæ´»ã€å¼ºå¤§ | éœ€è¦äººå·¥æŒ‡å¯¼ | å¤æ‚å®šç†ã€æ•°å­¦è¯æ˜ |
| **SMTæ±‚è§£** | ä¸€é˜¶é€»è¾‘+ç†è®º | æŒ‡æ•°æ—¶é—´ | å¤šé¡¹å¼ç©ºé—´ | é«˜æ•ˆã€å®ç”¨ | ä¸å®Œå¤‡ | ç¨‹åºéªŒè¯ã€çº¦æŸæ±‚è§£ |

**ç¬¦å·è¯´æ˜**ï¼š

- æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šæœ€åæƒ…å†µä¸‹çš„æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦
- ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šæœ€åæƒ…å†µä¸‹çš„ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦

### 3.1 å½’ç»“åŸç† / Resolution Principle

**å®šä¹‰ 3.1** (å½’ç»“åŸç† / Resolution Principle)
**å½’ç»“åŸç†**æ˜¯è‡ªåŠ¨å®šç†è¯æ˜çš„åŸºç¡€ï¼š
$$\frac{A \lor B \quad \neg A \lor C}{B \lor C}$$

**ç®—æ³• 3.1** (å½’ç»“ç®—æ³• / Resolution Algorithm)

```python
class ResolutionProver:
    def __init__(self, clauses):
        self.clauses = clauses
        self.resolvents = set()
        self.proof_steps = []

    def prove(self):
        """æ‰§è¡Œå½’ç»“è¯æ˜"""
        while True:
            # é€‰æ‹©ä¸¤ä¸ªå­å¥è¿›è¡Œå½’ç»“
            new_resolvents = set()

            for clause1 in self.clauses:
                for clause2 in self.clauses:
                    if clause1 != clause2:
                        resolvent = self.resolve(clause1, clause2)
                        if resolvent is not None:
                            new_resolvents.add(resolvent)

                            # è®°å½•è¯æ˜æ­¥éª¤
                            self.proof_steps.append({
                                'clause1': clause1,
                                'clause2': clause2,
                                'resolvent': resolvent
                            })

            # æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦å¾—åˆ°ç©ºå­å¥
            if frozenset() in new_resolvents:
                return {
                    'success': True,
                    'proof': self.proof_steps
                }

            # æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦æœ‰æ–°çš„å½’ç»“å¼
            if new_resolvents.issubset(self.resolvents):
                return {
                    'success': False,
                    'reason': 'No new resolvents generated'
                }

            # æ·»åŠ æ–°çš„å½’ç»“å¼
            self.resolvents.update(new_resolvents)
            self.clauses.update(new_resolvents)

    def resolve(self, clause1, clause2):
        """å½’ç»“ä¸¤ä¸ªå­å¥"""
        # å¯»æ‰¾äº’è¡¥æ–‡å­—
        for literal1 in clause1:
            for literal2 in clause2:
                if self.is_complementary(literal1, literal2):
                    # åˆ›å»ºå½’ç»“å¼
                    resolvent = set()
                    resolvent.update(clause1 - {literal1})
                    resolvent.update(clause2 - {literal2})
                    return frozenset(resolvent)
        return None

    def is_complementary(self, literal1, literal2):
        """åˆ¤æ–­ä¸¤ä¸ªæ–‡å­—æ˜¯å¦äº’è¡¥"""
        return literal1 == Negation(literal2) or literal2 == Negation(literal1)
```

**ç¤ºä¾‹ 3.1** (å½’ç»“è¯æ˜ç¤ºä¾‹)

```python
# è¯æ˜ï¼šä» {p âˆ¨ q, Â¬p âˆ¨ r, Â¬q âˆ¨ s} å¯ä»¥æ¨å¯¼å‡º r âˆ¨ s
clauses = [
    frozenset(['p', 'q']),      # p âˆ¨ q
    frozenset(['Â¬p', 'r']),     # Â¬p âˆ¨ r
    frozenset(['Â¬q', 's'])      # Â¬q âˆ¨ s
]

prover = ResolutionProver(clauses)
result = prover.prove()
print("å½’ç»“è¯æ˜ç»“æœï¼š", result)
```

### 3.2 æ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹ / Model Checking

**å®šä¹‰ 3.2** (æ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹ / Model Checking)
**æ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹**æ˜¯è‡ªåŠ¨éªŒè¯ç³»ç»Ÿæ€§è´¨çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼š
$$M \models \phi$$
å…¶ä¸­ $M$ æ˜¯ç³»ç»Ÿæ¨¡å‹ï¼Œ$\phi$ æ˜¯æ€§è´¨ã€‚

**å®šä¹‰ 3.3** (Kripkeç»“æ„ / Kripke Structure)
**Kripkeç»“æ„**æ˜¯æ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹çš„å½¢å¼åŒ–æ¨¡å‹ï¼š
$$K = (S, S_0, R, L)$$
å…¶ä¸­ï¼š

- $S$ æ˜¯**çŠ¶æ€é›†**ï¼ˆstate setï¼‰
- $S_0 \subseteq S$ æ˜¯**åˆå§‹çŠ¶æ€é›†**ï¼ˆinitial state setï¼‰
- $R \subseteq S \times S$ æ˜¯**è½¬ç§»å…³ç³»**ï¼ˆtransition relationï¼‰
- $L: S \to 2^{AP}$ æ˜¯**æ ‡è®°å‡½æ•°**ï¼ˆlabeling functionï¼‰

**ç®—æ³• 3.2** (æ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹ç®—æ³• / Model Checking Algorithm)

```python
class ModelChecker:
    def __init__(self, kripke_structure):
        self.kripke = kripke_structure
        self.satisfaction_sets = {}

    def check(self, formula):
        """æ£€æŸ¥Kripkeç»“æ„æ˜¯å¦æ»¡è¶³å…¬å¼"""
        if isinstance(formula, AtomicProposition):
            return self.check_atomic(formula)
        elif isinstance(formula, Negation):
            return self.check_negation(formula)
        elif isinstance(formula, Conjunction):
            return self.check_conjunction(formula)
        elif isinstance(formula, Disjunction):
            return self.check_disjunction(formula)
        elif isinstance(formula, Always):
            return self.check_always(formula)
        elif isinstance(formula, Eventually):
            return self.check_eventually(formula)
        elif isinstance(formula, Next):
            return self.check_next(formula)
        elif isinstance(formula, Until):
            return self.check_until(formula)

    def check_atomic(self, formula):
        """æ£€æŸ¥åŸå­å‘½é¢˜"""
        return {s for s in self.kripke.states
                if formula.prop in self.kripke.labels[s]}

    def check_negation(self, formula):
        """æ£€æŸ¥å¦å®šå…¬å¼"""
        sat_set = self.check(formula.operand)
        return self.kripke.states - sat_set

    def check_conjunction(self, formula):
        """æ£€æŸ¥åˆå–å…¬å¼"""
        sat_set1 = self.check(formula.left)
        sat_set2 = self.check(formula.right)
        return sat_set1 & sat_set2

    def check_disjunction(self, formula):
        """æ£€æŸ¥æå–å…¬å¼"""
        sat_set1 = self.check(formula.left)
        sat_set2 = self.check(formula.right)
        return sat_set1 | sat_set2

    def check_always(self, formula):
        """æ£€æŸ¥æ€»æ˜¯å…¬å¼ GÏ†"""
        # ä½¿ç”¨ä¸åŠ¨ç‚¹ç®—æ³•
        sat_set = self.kripke.states
        while True:
            new_sat_set = sat_set & self.check_next(Always(formula.operand))
            if new_sat_set == sat_set:
                break
            sat_set = new_sat_set
        return sat_set

    def check_eventually(self, formula):
        """æ£€æŸ¥æœ€ç»ˆå…¬å¼ FÏ†"""
        # ä½¿ç”¨ä¸åŠ¨ç‚¹ç®—æ³•
        sat_set = set()
        while True:
            new_sat_set = sat_set | self.check(formula.operand) | self.check_next(Eventually(formula.operand))
            if new_sat_set == sat_set:
                break
            sat_set = new_sat_set
        return sat_set

    def check_next(self, formula):
        """æ£€æŸ¥ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªå…¬å¼ XÏ†"""
        sat_set = self.check(formula.operand)
        return {s for s in self.kripke.states
                if all(t in sat_set for t in self.kripke.transitions.get(s, []))}

    def check_until(self, formula):
        """æ£€æŸ¥ç›´åˆ°å…¬å¼ Ï† U Ïˆ"""
        # ä½¿ç”¨ä¸åŠ¨ç‚¹ç®—æ³•
        sat_set = set()
        psi_set = self.check(formula.right)

        while True:
            new_sat_set = psi_set | (self.check(formula.left) & self.check_next(Until(formula.left, formula.right)))
            if new_sat_set == sat_set:
                break
            sat_set = new_sat_set
        return sat_set
```

**ç¤ºä¾‹ 3.2** (æ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹ç¤ºä¾‹)

```python
# å®šä¹‰Kripkeç»“æ„
states = {'s0', 's1', 's2'}
initial_states = {'s0'}
transitions = {
    's0': ['s1'],
    's1': ['s2'],
    's2': ['s0']
}
labels = {
    's0': {'p'},
    's1': {'q'},
    's2': {'p', 'q'}
}

kripke = KripkeStructure(states, initial_states, transitions, labels)
checker = ModelChecker(kripke)

# æ£€æŸ¥æ€§è´¨ï¼šG(p âˆ¨ q)
formula = Always(Disjunction(AtomicProposition('p'), AtomicProposition('q')))
result = checker.check(formula)
print("æ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹ç»“æœï¼š", result)
```

### 3.2 å®šç†è¯æ˜

**å®šä¹‰ 3.3** (å®šç†è¯æ˜å™¨)
**å®šç†è¯æ˜å™¨**æ˜¯è‡ªåŠ¨è¯æ˜æ•°å­¦å®šç†çš„ç³»ç»Ÿï¼š
$$
\text{prover}(\phi) = \begin{cases}
\text{valid} & \text{if } \vdash \phi \\
\text{invalid} & \text{otherwise}
\end{cases}
$$

**ç®—æ³• 3.2** (å½’ç»“è¯æ˜)

```text
è¾“å…¥ï¼šå…¬å¼é›† Fï¼Œç›®æ ‡ç»“è®º C
è¾“å‡ºï¼šè¯æ˜ç»“æœ

1. è½¬æ¢ä¸ºCNFï¼šclauses = convert_to_cnf(F âˆª {Â¬C})
2. å½’ç»“è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼šwhile not empty(clauses) do
   a. é€‰æ‹©å­å¥å¯¹ï¼šc1, c2 = select_clauses(clauses)
   b. å½’ç»“ï¼šresolvent = resolve(c1, c2)
   c. å¦‚æœå¾—åˆ°ç©ºå­å¥ï¼šif resolvent is empty then
      return "valid"
   d. æ·»åŠ å½’ç»“å¼ï¼šclauses.add(resolvent)
3. è¿”å›ç»“æœï¼šreturn "invalid"
```

## ğŸ’» **4. ç¨‹åºéªŒè¯ / Program Verification**

### 4.0 ç¨‹åºéªŒè¯æ–¹æ³•å¯¹æ¯”çŸ©é˜µ / Program Verification Methods Comparison Matrix

| æ–¹æ³• | éªŒè¯å¯¹è±¡ | éªŒè¯æ€§è´¨ | è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–ç¨‹åº¦ | ä¼˜ç‚¹ | ç¼ºç‚¹ | å…¸å‹åº”ç”¨ |
|------|---------|---------|-----------|------|------|---------|
| **Hoareé€»è¾‘** | å‘½ä»¤å¼ç¨‹åº | éƒ¨åˆ†æ­£ç¡®æ€§ | åŠè‡ªåŠ¨ | ç†è®ºåŸºç¡€å¼ºã€ç³»ç»ŸåŒ– | éœ€è¦å¾ªç¯ä¸å˜é‡ | ç®—æ³•éªŒè¯ |
| **åˆ†ç¦»é€»è¾‘** | æŒ‡é’ˆç¨‹åº | å†…å­˜å®‰å…¨ | åŠè‡ªåŠ¨ | å¤„ç†æŒ‡é’ˆã€å¹¶å‘ | å¤æ‚ã€éœ€è¦åˆ†ç¦»æ€æƒ³ | ç³»ç»Ÿç¨‹åºéªŒè¯ |
| **ç±»å‹ç³»ç»Ÿ** | å‡½æ•°å¼ç¨‹åº | ç±»å‹å®‰å…¨ | å…¨è‡ªåŠ¨ | ç¼–è¯‘æ—¶æ£€æŸ¥ã€é«˜æ•ˆ | è¡¨è¾¾èƒ½åŠ›æœ‰é™ | å‡½æ•°å¼è¯­è¨€ |
| **æ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹** | å¹¶å‘ç³»ç»Ÿ | æ—¶æ€æ€§è´¨ | å…¨è‡ªåŠ¨ | è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–ã€åä¾‹ç”Ÿæˆ | çŠ¶æ€ç©ºé—´çˆ†ç‚¸ | åè®®éªŒè¯ |
| **æŠ½è±¡è§£é‡Š** | ç¨‹åºåˆ†æ | è¿è¡Œæ—¶æ€§è´¨ | å…¨è‡ªåŠ¨ | é«˜æ•ˆã€å¯æ‰©å±• | å¯èƒ½ä¸ç²¾ç¡® | é™æ€åˆ†æ |
| **ç¬¦å·æ‰§è¡Œ** | ç¨‹åºè·¯å¾„ | è·¯å¾„æ€§è´¨ | åŠè‡ªåŠ¨ | ç²¾ç¡®ã€è·¯å¾„è¦†ç›– | è·¯å¾„çˆ†ç‚¸ | æµ‹è¯•ç”Ÿæˆ |

### 4.1 Hoareé€»è¾‘ / Hoare Logic

**å®šä¹‰ 4.1** (Hoareä¸‰å…ƒç»„ / Hoare Triple)
**Hoareä¸‰å…ƒç»„**æè¿°ç¨‹åºçš„å‰ç½®å’Œåç½®æ¡ä»¶ï¼š
$$\{P\} C \{Q\}$$
å…¶ä¸­ï¼š

- $P$ æ˜¯**å‰ç½®æ¡ä»¶**ï¼ˆpreconditionï¼‰
- $C$ æ˜¯**ç¨‹åºä»£ç **ï¼ˆprogram codeï¼‰
- $Q$ æ˜¯**åç½®æ¡ä»¶**ï¼ˆpostconditionï¼‰

**è¯­ä¹‰å®šä¹‰**ï¼š
$$\{P\} C \{Q\} \iff \forall \sigma: \sigma \models P \land \sigma' = \llbracket C \rrbracket(\sigma) \implies \sigma' \models Q$$

å…¶ä¸­ $\sigma$ æ˜¯ç¨‹åºçŠ¶æ€ï¼Œ$\llbracket C \rrbracket$ æ˜¯ç¨‹åº $C$ çš„è¯­ä¹‰å‡½æ•°ã€‚

**Hoareé€»è¾‘è§„åˆ™**ï¼š

**èµ‹å€¼è§„åˆ™**ï¼š
$$\frac{}{\{P[E/x]\} x := E \{P\}}$$

**å®šç† 4.1.1** (èµ‹å€¼è§„åˆ™çš„æ­£ç¡®æ€§ / Assignment Rule Correctness)
èµ‹å€¼è§„åˆ™æ˜¯æ­£ç¡®çš„ã€‚

**è¯æ˜**ï¼š

- å¦‚æœæ‰§è¡Œèµ‹å€¼ $x := E$ å‰çŠ¶æ€ $\sigma$ æ»¡è¶³ $P[E/x]$ï¼Œåˆ™ $\sigma(x) = E$ çš„å€¼
- æ‰§è¡Œèµ‹å€¼åï¼ŒçŠ¶æ€ $\sigma'$ æ»¡è¶³ $\sigma'(x) = \llbracket E \rrbracket(\sigma)$
- ç”±äº $\sigma \models P[E/x]$ï¼Œä¸” $P[E/x]$ æ˜¯å°† $P$ ä¸­çš„ $x$ æ›¿æ¢ä¸º $E$ å¾—åˆ°çš„ï¼Œå› æ­¤ $\sigma' \models P$
- å› æ­¤ï¼Œ$\{P[E/x]\} x := E \{P\}$ æˆç«‹ $\square$

**åºåˆ—è§„åˆ™**ï¼š
$$\frac{\{P\} C_1 \{R\} \quad \{R\} C_2 \{Q\}}{\{P\} C_1; C_2 \{Q\}}$$

**å®šç† 4.1.2** (åºåˆ—è§„åˆ™çš„æ­£ç¡®æ€§ / Sequence Rule Correctness)
åºåˆ—è§„åˆ™æ˜¯æ­£ç¡®çš„ã€‚

**è¯æ˜**ï¼š

- å¦‚æœ $\{P\} C_1 \{R\}$ å’Œ $\{R\} C_2 \{Q\}$ éƒ½æˆç«‹
- å¯¹äºæ»¡è¶³ $P$ çš„çŠ¶æ€ $\sigma$ï¼Œæ‰§è¡Œ $C_1$ åå¾—åˆ°çŠ¶æ€ $\sigma_1$ æ»¡è¶³ $R$
- æ‰§è¡Œ $C_2$ åå¾—åˆ°çŠ¶æ€ $\sigma_2$ æ»¡è¶³ $Q$
- å› æ­¤ï¼Œ$\{P\} C_1; C_2 \{Q\}$ æˆç«‹ $\square$

**æ¡ä»¶è§„åˆ™**ï¼š
$$\frac{\{P \land B\} C_1 \{Q\} \quad \{P \land \neg B\} C_2 \{Q\}}{\{P\} \text{if } B \text{ then } C_1 \text{ else } C_2 \{Q\}}$$

**å®šç† 4.1.3** (æ¡ä»¶è§„åˆ™çš„æ­£ç¡®æ€§ / Conditional Rule Correctness)
æ¡ä»¶è§„åˆ™æ˜¯æ­£ç¡®çš„ã€‚

**è¯æ˜**ï¼š

- å¦‚æœ $\{P \land B\} C_1 \{Q\}$ å’Œ $\{P \land \neg B\} C_2 \{Q\}$ éƒ½æˆç«‹
- å¯¹äºæ»¡è¶³ $P$ çš„çŠ¶æ€ $\sigma$ï¼š
  - å¦‚æœ $\sigma \models B$ï¼Œåˆ™æ‰§è¡Œ $C_1$ï¼Œç”± $\{P \land B\} C_1 \{Q\}$ï¼Œç»“æœæ»¡è¶³ $Q$
  - å¦‚æœ $\sigma \models \neg B$ï¼Œåˆ™æ‰§è¡Œ $C_2$ï¼Œç”± $\{P \land \neg B\} C_2 \{Q\}$ï¼Œç»“æœæ»¡è¶³ $Q$
- å› æ­¤ï¼Œ$\{P\} \text{if } B \text{ then } C_1 \text{ else } C_2 \{Q\}$ æˆç«‹ $\square$

**å¾ªç¯è§„åˆ™**ï¼š
$$\frac{\{P \land B\} C \{P\}}{\{P\} \text{while } B \text{ do } C \{P \land \neg B\}}$$

**å®šç† 4.1.4** (å¾ªç¯è§„åˆ™çš„æ­£ç¡®æ€§ / While Rule Correctness)
å¾ªç¯è§„åˆ™æ˜¯æ­£ç¡®çš„ï¼ˆéƒ¨åˆ†æ­£ç¡®æ€§ï¼‰ã€‚

**è¯æ˜**ï¼š

- å¦‚æœ $\{P \land B\} C \{P\}$ æˆç«‹ï¼Œåˆ™ $P$ æ˜¯å¾ªç¯ä¸å˜é‡
- å¯¹äºæ»¡è¶³ $P$ çš„çŠ¶æ€ $\sigma$ï¼š
  - å¦‚æœ $\sigma \models \neg B$ï¼Œå¾ªç¯ä¸æ‰§è¡Œï¼ŒçŠ¶æ€ä»æ»¡è¶³ $P \land \neg B$
  - å¦‚æœ $\sigma \models B$ï¼Œæ‰§è¡Œ $C$ ä¸€æ¬¡ï¼Œç”±å¾ªç¯ä¸å˜é‡ï¼Œç»“æœä»æ»¡è¶³ $P$
  - é‡å¤ä¸Šè¿°è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼Œç›´åˆ° $B$ ä¸ºå‡
- ç”±äºæ˜¯éƒ¨åˆ†æ­£ç¡®æ€§ï¼Œå‡è®¾å¾ªç¯ç»ˆæ­¢ï¼Œæœ€ç»ˆçŠ¶æ€æ»¡è¶³ $P \land \neg B$
- å› æ­¤ï¼Œ$\{P\} \text{while } B \text{ do } C \{P \land \neg B\}$ æˆç«‹ $\square$

**æ³¨æ„**ï¼šå¾ªç¯è§„åˆ™åªä¿è¯éƒ¨åˆ†æ­£ç¡®æ€§ï¼ˆpartial correctnessï¼‰ï¼Œå³å¦‚æœå¾ªç¯ç»ˆæ­¢ï¼Œåˆ™åç½®æ¡ä»¶æˆç«‹ã€‚è¦ä¿è¯å®Œå…¨æ­£ç¡®æ€§ï¼ˆtotal correctnessï¼‰ï¼Œè¿˜éœ€è¦è¯æ˜å¾ªç¯ç»ˆæ­¢ã€‚

**ç®—æ³• 4.1** (Hoareé€»è¾‘éªŒè¯å™¨ / Hoare Logic Verifier)

```python
class HoareVerifier:
    def __init__(self):
        self.rules = {
            'assignment': self.assignment_rule,
            'sequence': self.sequence_rule,
            'conditional': self.conditional_rule,
            'loop': self.loop_rule
        }

    def verify(self, precondition, program, postcondition):
        """éªŒè¯Hoareä¸‰å…ƒç»„"""
        if isinstance(program, Assignment):
            return self.verify_assignment(precondition, program, postcondition)
        elif isinstance(program, Sequence):
            return self.verify_sequence(precondition, program, postcondition)
        elif isinstance(program, Conditional):
            return self.verify_conditional(precondition, program, postcondition)
        elif isinstance(program, Loop):
            return self.verify_loop(precondition, program, postcondition)

    def verify_assignment(self, precondition, assignment, postcondition):
        """éªŒè¯èµ‹å€¼è¯­å¥"""
        # åº”ç”¨èµ‹å€¼è§„åˆ™
        substituted_pre = self.substitute(postcondition, assignment.variable, assignment.expression)
        return self.entails(precondition, substituted_pre)

    def verify_sequence(self, precondition, sequence, postcondition):
        """éªŒè¯åºåˆ—è¯­å¥"""
        # å¯»æ‰¾ä¸­é—´æ–­è¨€
        intermediate = self.find_intermediate_assertion(precondition, sequence, postcondition)

        # éªŒè¯ä¸¤ä¸ªéƒ¨åˆ†
        first_valid = self.verify(precondition, sequence.first, intermediate)
        second_valid = self.verify(intermediate, sequence.second, postcondition)

        return first_valid and second_valid

    def verify_conditional(self, precondition, conditional, postcondition):
        """éªŒè¯æ¡ä»¶è¯­å¥"""
        # éªŒè¯thenåˆ†æ”¯
        then_valid = self.verify(
            self.conjoin(precondition, conditional.condition),
            conditional.then_branch,
            postcondition
        )

        # éªŒè¯elseåˆ†æ”¯
        else_valid = self.verify(
            self.conjoin(precondition, self.negate(conditional.condition)),
            conditional.else_branch,
            postcondition
        )

        return then_valid and else_valid

    def verify_loop(self, precondition, loop, postcondition):
        """éªŒè¯å¾ªç¯è¯­å¥"""
        # å¯»æ‰¾å¾ªç¯ä¸å˜å¼
        invariant = self.find_loop_invariant(precondition, loop, postcondition)

        # éªŒè¯å¾ªç¯ä¸å˜å¼
        invariant_valid = self.entails(precondition, invariant)

        # éªŒè¯å¾ªç¯ä½“ä¿æŒä¸å˜å¼
        body_valid = self.verify(
            self.conjoin(invariant, loop.condition),
            loop.body,
            invariant
        )

        # éªŒè¯åç½®æ¡ä»¶
        post_valid = self.entails(
            self.conjoin(invariant, self.negate(loop.condition)),
            postcondition
        )

        return invariant_valid and body_valid and post_valid
```

**ç¤ºä¾‹ 4.1** (Hoareé€»è¾‘éªŒè¯ç¤ºä¾‹)

```python
# éªŒè¯ç¨‹åºï¼šx := x + 1; y := y + 1
program = Sequence(
    Assignment('x', Add(Variable('x'), Constant(1))),
    Assignment('y', Add(Variable('y'), Constant(1)))
)

precondition = And(Equal(Variable('x'), Constant(5)), Equal(Variable('y'), Constant(3)))
postcondition = And(Equal(Variable('x'), Constant(6)), Equal(Variable('y'), Constant(4)))

verifier = HoareVerifier()
result = verifier.verify(precondition, program, postcondition)
print("Hoareé€»è¾‘éªŒè¯ç»“æœï¼š", result)
```

å…¶ä¸­ï¼š

- $P$ æ˜¯å‰ç½®æ¡ä»¶
- $C$ æ˜¯ç¨‹åº
- $Q$ æ˜¯åç½®æ¡ä»¶

**å®šä¹‰ 4.2** (èµ‹å€¼å…¬ç†)
**èµ‹å€¼å…¬ç†**ï¼š
$$\{P[E/x]\} x := E \{P\}$$

**å®šä¹‰ 4.3** (åºåˆ—è§„åˆ™)
**åºåˆ—è§„åˆ™**ï¼š
$$\frac{\{P\} C_1 \{R\} \quad \{R\} C_2 \{Q\}}{\{P\} C_1; C_2 \{Q\}}$$

**å®šä¹‰ 4.4** (æ¡ä»¶è§„åˆ™)
**æ¡ä»¶è§„åˆ™**ï¼š
$$\frac{\{P \land B\} C_1 \{Q\} \quad \{P \land \neg B\} C_2 \{Q\}}{\{P\} \text{if } B \text{ then } C_1 \text{ else } C_2 \{Q\}}$$

**å®šä¹‰ 4.5** (å¾ªç¯è§„åˆ™)
**å¾ªç¯è§„åˆ™**ï¼š
$$\frac{\{P \land B\} C \{P\}}{\{P\} \text{while } B \text{ do } C \{P \land \neg B\}}$$

### 4.2 æœ€å¼±å‰ç½®æ¡ä»¶

**å®šä¹‰ 4.6** (æœ€å¼±å‰ç½®æ¡ä»¶)
**æœ€å¼±å‰ç½®æ¡ä»¶**æ˜¯ä½¿ç¨‹åºæ‰§è¡Œåæ»¡è¶³åç½®æ¡ä»¶çš„æœ€å¼±å‰ç½®æ¡ä»¶ï¼š
$$\text{wp}(C, Q) = \{s : \text{æ‰§è¡Œ } C \text{ ä» } s \text{ å¼€å§‹ï¼Œæœ€ç»ˆçŠ¶æ€æ»¡è¶³ } Q\}$$

**ç®—æ³• 4.1** (æœ€å¼±å‰ç½®æ¡ä»¶è®¡ç®—)

```text
è¾“å…¥ï¼šç¨‹åº Cï¼Œåç½®æ¡ä»¶ Q
è¾“å‡ºï¼šæœ€å¼±å‰ç½®æ¡ä»¶

1. æ ¹æ®ç¨‹åºç»“æ„è®¡ç®—ï¼š
   a. èµ‹å€¼ï¼šwp(x := E, Q) = Q[E/x]
   b. åºåˆ—ï¼šwp(C1; C2, Q) = wp(C1, wp(C2, Q))
   c. æ¡ä»¶ï¼šwp(if B then C1 else C2, Q) =
      (B âˆ§ wp(C1, Q)) âˆ¨ (Â¬B âˆ§ wp(C2, Q))
   d. å¾ªç¯ï¼šwp(while B do C, Q) =
      âˆƒk. wp(loop_k, Q)
2. è¿”å›ç»“æœï¼šreturn wp(C, Q)
```

## 5. ç±»å‹ç³»ç»Ÿ

### 5.1 ç®€å•ç±»å‹ç³»ç»Ÿ

**å®šä¹‰ 5.1** (ç±»å‹)
**ç±»å‹**æ˜¯å€¼çš„é›†åˆï¼š
$$\tau ::= \text{bool} \mid \text{int} \mid \tau_1 \to \tau_2$$

**å®šä¹‰ 5.2** (ç±»å‹ç¯å¢ƒ)
**ç±»å‹ç¯å¢ƒ**æ˜¯å˜é‡åˆ°ç±»å‹çš„æ˜ å°„ï¼š

**ç®—æ³• 5.1** (ç±»å‹æ£€æŸ¥ç®—æ³•)

### 5.2 å¤šæ€ç±»å‹ç³»ç»Ÿ

## 6. å¹¶å‘éªŒè¯

### 6.1 çº¿æ€§æ—¶åºé€»è¾‘

**å®šä¹‰ 6.1** (LTLå…¬å¼)
**çº¿æ€§æ—¶åºé€»è¾‘** (LTL) å…¬å¼ï¼š
$$\phi ::= p \mid \neg \phi \mid \phi_1 \land \phi_2 \mid \mathbf{X} \phi \mid \mathbf{F} \phi \mid \mathbf{G} \phi \mid \phi_1 \mathbf{U} \phi_2$$

å…¶ä¸­ï¼š

- $\mathbf{X}$ æ˜¯ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªæ—¶é—´ç‚¹
- $\mathbf{F}$ æ˜¯å°†æ¥æŸä¸ªæ—¶é—´ç‚¹
- $\mathbf{G}$ æ˜¯å°†æ¥æ‰€æœ‰æ—¶é—´ç‚¹
- $\mathbf{U}$ æ˜¯ç›´åˆ°

**å®šä¹‰ 6.2** (LTLè¯­ä¹‰)
**LTLè¯­ä¹‰**ï¼š
$$\pi, i \models \mathbf{X} \phi \iff \pi, i+1 \models \phi$$
$$\pi, i \models \mathbf{F} \phi \iff \exists j \geq i: \pi, j \models \phi$$
$$\pi, i \models \mathbf{G} \phi \iff \forall j \geq i: \pi, j \models \phi$$

### 6.2 è®¡ç®—æ ‘é€»è¾‘

**å®šä¹‰ 6.3** (CTLå…¬å¼)
**è®¡ç®—æ ‘é€»è¾‘** (CTL) å…¬å¼ï¼š
$$\phi ::= p \mid \neg \phi \mid \phi_1 \land \phi_2 \mid \mathbf{EX} \phi \mid \mathbf{EF} \phi \mid \mathbf{EG} \phi \mid \mathbf{E}[\phi_1 \mathbf{U} \phi_2]$$

**ç®—æ³• 6.1** (CTLæ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹)

```text
è¾“å…¥ï¼šKripkeç»“æ„ Kï¼ŒCTLå…¬å¼ Ï†
è¾“å‡ºï¼šæ»¡è¶³ Ï† çš„çŠ¶æ€é›†

1. é€’å½’è®¡ç®—ï¼š
   a. åŸå­å‘½é¢˜ï¼šSat(p) = {s : p âˆˆ L(s)}
   b. å¦å®šï¼šSat(Â¬Ï†) = S - Sat(Ï†)
   c. åˆå–ï¼šSat(Ï†1âˆ§Ï†2) = Sat(Ï†1) âˆ© Sat(Ï†2)
   d. EXï¼šSat(EX Ï†) = {s : âˆƒt. (s,t) âˆˆ R âˆ§ t âˆˆ Sat(Ï†)}
   e. EFï¼šSat(EF Ï†) = least_fixed_point(Î»X. Sat(Ï†) âˆª Sat(EX X))
2. è¿”å›ç»“æœï¼šreturn Sat(Ï†)
```

## 7. ç¨‹åºåˆ†æ

### 7.1 æ•°æ®æµåˆ†æ

**å®šä¹‰ 7.1** (æ•°æ®æµåˆ†æ)
**æ•°æ®æµåˆ†æ**è®¡ç®—ç¨‹åºç‚¹çš„å±æ€§ï¼š
$$\text{in}(n) = \bigcup_{p \in \text{pred}(n)} \text{out}(p)$$
$$\text{out}(n) = f_n(\text{in}(n))$$

**ç®—æ³• 7.1** (è¿­ä»£æ•°æ®æµåˆ†æ)

```text
è¾“å…¥ï¼šæ§åˆ¶æµå›¾ CFGï¼Œè½¬ç§»å‡½æ•° f
è¾“å‡ºï¼šæ¯ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„ in/out é›†åˆ

1. åˆå§‹åŒ–ï¼šfor each node n do
   a. in[n] = âˆ…
   b. out[n] = âˆ…
2. è¿­ä»£ï¼šrepeat until no change
   a. for each node n do
      i. in[n] = âˆª{out[p] : p âˆˆ pred(n)}
      ii. out[n] = f_n(in[n])
3. è¿”å›ç»“æœï¼šreturn in, out
```

### 7.2 æŠ½è±¡è§£é‡Š

**å®šä¹‰ 7.2** (æŠ½è±¡åŸŸ)
**æŠ½è±¡åŸŸ**æ˜¯å…·ä½“åŸŸçš„æŠ½è±¡ï¼š
$$\mathcal{A} = \langle A, \sqsubseteq, \sqcup, \sqcap, \bot, \top \rangle$$

**å®šä¹‰ 7.3** (æŠ½è±¡å‡½æ•°)

è¾“å‡ºï¼šæŠ½è±¡è¯­ä¹‰

   a. abstract_state = âŠ¥

## 8. è¯æ˜è¾…åŠ©å·¥å…·

### 8.1 è¯æ˜ç­–ç•¥

**å®šä¹‰ 8.1** (è¯æ˜ç­–ç•¥)
**è¯æ˜ç­–ç•¥**æ˜¯è‡ªåŠ¨è¯æ˜çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼š

### 8.2 è¯æ˜æœç´¢

**å®šä¹‰ 8.2** (è¯æ˜æœç´¢)
**è¯æ˜æœç´¢**æ˜¯å¯»æ‰¾è¯æ˜çš„è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼š

## 1. å½¢å¼åŒ–è¯æ˜çš„æ¦‚å¿µã€å®šä¹‰ä¸è§£é‡Š

### 1.1 æ¦‚å¿µ

### 8.5 ä¼¦ç†ã€å¯è§£é‡Šæ€§ä¸ç¤¾ä¼šå½±å“

å¦‚éœ€æŸä¸€ä¸“é¢˜çš„æ›´æ·±å±‚æ¡ˆä¾‹ã€è·¨é¢†åŸŸå·¥ç¨‹æ¨¡æ¿æˆ–æœªæ¥ç ”ç©¶è·¯çº¿å›¾ï¼Œè¯·ç»§ç»­æŒ‡å®šï¼

## 0.5 å„åˆ†æ”¯å…¸å‹å½¢å¼åŒ–å®šä¹‰ä¸å¤šè¡¨å¾å®ä¾‹ï¼ˆé€’å½’è¡¥å…¨ï¼‰

### å›¾è®ºåŸºç¡€

- **å®šä¹‰ï¼ˆç¬¦å·ï¼‰**ï¼š$G=(V,E)$ï¼Œ$V$ä¸ºèŠ‚ç‚¹é›†ï¼Œ$E\subseteq V\times V$ä¸ºè¾¹é›†ã€‚
- **ç»“æ„å›¾**ï¼š

```mermaid
graph TD;
  A--B;
  B--C;
  C--A;
```

- **æ€§è´¨è¯æ˜ï¼ˆå½’çº³æ³•ï¼‰**ï¼š
  - å‘½é¢˜ï¼šä»»æ„è¿é€šæ— å‘å›¾å­˜åœ¨ç”Ÿæˆæ ‘ã€‚
  - è¯æ˜ï¼šå¯¹èŠ‚ç‚¹æ•°å½’çº³ï¼Œ$n=1$æ—¶æˆç«‹ï¼Œå‡è®¾$n=k$æˆç«‹ï¼Œ$n=k+1$æ—¶å»é™¤ä¸€æ¡è¾¹ï¼Œå½’çº³å¾—è¯ã€‚
- **è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–è„šæœ¬ï¼ˆNetworkXï¼‰**ï¼š

```python
import networkx as nx
G = nx.Graph([("A","B"),("B","C"),("C","A")])
assert nx.is_connected(G)
```

### ç½‘ç»œæ‹“æ‰‘

- **å®šä¹‰ï¼ˆç¬¦å·ï¼‰**ï¼šæ‹“æ‰‘$T=(N,L)$ï¼Œ$N$ä¸ºèŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œ$L$ä¸ºé“¾è·¯ã€‚
- **å±‚æ¬¡ç»“æ„å›¾**ï¼š

```mermaid
graph TD;
  Core-->Layer1;
  Layer1-->Layer2;
```

- **æ€§è´¨è¯æ˜ï¼ˆæ„é€ æ³•ï¼‰**ï¼š
  - å‘½é¢˜ï¼šæ˜Ÿå‹æ‹“æ‰‘çš„ä¸­å¿ƒèŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸ºå‰²ç‚¹ã€‚
  - è¯æ˜ï¼šç§»é™¤ä¸­å¿ƒèŠ‚ç‚¹åç½‘ç»œä¸è¿é€šï¼Œè¯æ¯•ã€‚
- **è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–è„šæœ¬ï¼ˆPythonï¼‰**ï¼š

```python
# æ£€æŸ¥å‰²ç‚¹
import networkx as nx
G = nx.star_graph(4)
assert list(nx.articulation_points(G)) == [0]
```

### é€šä¿¡åè®®

- **å®šä¹‰ï¼ˆè‡ªåŠ¨æœºç¬¦å·ï¼‰**ï¼š$A=(Q,\Sigma,\delta,q_0,F)$ã€‚
- **çŠ¶æ€æœºå›¾**ï¼š

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> Idle
  Idle --> Sending : send
  Sending --> Idle : ack
```

- **æ­»é”æ€§è´¨è¯æ˜ï¼ˆæ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹ï¼‰**ï¼š
  - å‘½é¢˜ï¼šæ— æ­»é”åè®®ã€‚
  - è¯æ˜ï¼šç”¨TLA+éå†æ‰€æœ‰çŠ¶æ€ï¼Œæ— æ­»é”çŠ¶æ€ã€‚
- **è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–è„šæœ¬ï¼ˆTLA+ï¼‰**ï¼š

```tla
VARIABLES s
Init == s = "Idle"
Next == \/ (s = "Idle" /\ s' = "Sending")
         \/ (s = "Sending" /\ s' = "Idle")
Spec == Init /\ [][Next]_s
```

### åˆ†å¸ƒå¼ç³»ç»Ÿ

- **å®šä¹‰ï¼ˆäº‹ä»¶ç»“æ„ï¼‰**ï¼š$E=(Ev,\leq,\#$)$ï¼Œ$Ev$ä¸ºäº‹ä»¶é›†ï¼Œ$\leq$ä¸ºå› æœåºï¼Œ$\#$ä¸ºå†²çªå…³ç³»ã€‚
- **äº‹ä»¶ç»“æ„å›¾**ï¼š

- **ä¸€è‡´æ€§è¯æ˜ï¼ˆå½’çº³+æ¨¡å‹æ£€æµ‹ï¼‰**ï¼š
  - å‘½é¢˜ï¼šPaxosåè®®ä¿è¯ä¸€è‡´æ€§ã€‚

### é‡å­é€šä¿¡

  - è‡ªåŠ¨è¯†åˆ«çŸ¥è¯†ç©ºç™½ã€å†²çªä¸å†—ä½™ï¼Œè§¦å‘é€’å½’è¡¥å…¨ä¸æ‰¹åˆ¤æ€§ä¼˜åŒ–ã€‚
- **æ¼”åŒ–ç®—æ³•ä¼ªä»£ç **ï¼š
